NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE OF APPOINTMENT OF LIQUIDATOR PURSUANT TO SECTION 516
Name of Company

:

Textile Eco Solutions Tamil Nadu Limited

Marine disposal of effluents, waste water generated, discharged by textile processing units and
common effluents treatment plants, presently not carrying on any business activity

Name and Address
of Liquidator

62, Appachi Nagar Main Road, Kongu Nagar, Tirupur-641 607
Shri P. Vidhyaprakash,
274/1, Ganapathypalayam Main Road, Veerapandi, Tirupur-641 605

Date of Appointment :

By whom Appointed :

Members at the Extraordinary General Meeting held on 7-1-2013

Chennai,
30th January 2013.

P. VIDHYAPRAKASH,
Liquidator.

Koruvada Srinivas alias Srinivas was born at West Godavari District, Andhra Pradesh as a Male Child to K. Gangaraju
on 9th July 1967 and now residing at Old No. 36, New No. 8, GR FL Bharatipuram 6th Street, Shenoy Nagar,
Chennai-600 030. After an Elaborate Sexual reassignment surgery, she has been living as a Femal (reference Dr. V.
Jayaraman, MS. MCH, MNAMS Dip NB. Ph.D FICS (Regn. No. 32070) Clinical Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College and
Hospital Chennai). The thorough clinical Examination under Dr. V. Jayaraman, M.S. M.Ch. MNAMS, Dip NB Ph. D FICS
shows that I could to treated as a female. K. Srinivas shall henceforth be known as K. Vijayalakshmi.

Chennai,
1st February 2013.

K. SRINIVAS.
